[30;1m236 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m237 | [0m[35mWhat does the ``entrypoint`` do, it would seem not so much, it creates an[0m
[30;1m238 | [0m[35mevent-loop and transfers control to the user. However, under the hood, the[0m
